intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:

context = {'recent_rejected': [{'plan': {'actions': [{'type': 'press_key', 'value': 'esc'}]}, 'reason': 'Reuse the tab'}]}
intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()
E           AttributeError: 'MemoryManager' object has no attribute 'get_user_profile'

        planner = ContextualPlanner(memory=mem)

            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()

tests\test_aegis_v3_2_ultimate_500.py:108: 
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _

self = <brain.contextual_planner.ContextualPlanner object at 0x000001EB07C10600>
user_input = 'What should I do?'
context = {'daily_history': [{'action_type': 'type_text', 'app': 'Calculator', 'app_category': 'general', 'command': '1 + 1', ..... '1 + 1', ...}, {'action_type': 'type_text', 'app': 'Calculator', 'app_category': 'general', 'command': '1 + 1', ...}]}
intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
>               events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
E               KeyError: 'timestamp'

        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.

        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"

        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})

                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "

                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "

            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []

intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
>               events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")

intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
>               events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")

self = <brain.contextual_planner.ContextualPlanner object at 0x000001EB08FCCC20>
user_input = 'test'
context = {'daily_history': [], 'rejected_actions': [{'reason': 'Reject clearing input'}], 'state': {}}
intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()
E           AttributeError: 'MemoryManager' object has no attribute 'get_user_profile'

        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()
E           AttributeError: 'MemoryManager' object has no attribute 'get_user_profile'

self = <brain.contextual_planner.ContextualPlanner object at 0x000001EB08FCE040>
user_input = 'test'
context = {'daily_history': [], 'rejected_actions': [{'reason': 'Prefer minimal summaries'}], 'state': {}}
intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()

                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,

        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """

            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})

                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"

        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()

tests\test_aegis_v3_3_ultimate_matrix.py:245: 
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _

self = <brain.contextual_planner.ContextualPlanner object at 0x000001EB08FFB3F0>
user_input = 'test'
context = {'daily_history': [], 'rejected_actions': [{'reason': 'Reject opening new tab'}], 'state': {}}
intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()
E           AttributeError: 'MemoryManager' object has no attribute 'get_user_profile'

            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()

self = <brain.contextual_planner.ContextualPlanner object at 0x000001EB07BFE890>
user_input = 'test'
context = {'daily_history': [], 'rejected_actions': [{'reason': 'Reject opening new tab'}], 'state': {}}
intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()

        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()
E           AttributeError: 'MemoryManager' object has no attribute 'get_user_profile'

            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()

tests\test_aegis_v3_3_ultimate_matrix.py:245: 
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _

self = <brain.contextual_planner.ContextualPlanner object at 0x000001EB09023700>
user_input = 'test'
context = {'daily_history': [], 'rejected_actions': [{'reason': 'Reject clearing input'}], 'state': {}}
intent_metadata = None

    def _build_enriched_prompt(
        self,
        user_input: str,
        context: dict[str, Any],
        intent_metadata: IntentMetadata | None = None,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Build a prompt enriched with system context for Gemini.
    
        All pre-processing is logged. Pre-processing only formats
        context for inclusion — it NEVER creates action plans.
        """
        parts: list[str] = []
        state = context.get("session_state") or {}
    
        # Aegis v3.5: Intent Intelligence Metadata
        if intent_metadata:
            parts.append(
                f"[INTENT CLASSIFICATION]\n"
                f"  Primary Intents: {', '.join(intent_metadata.intent_types)}\n"
                f"  Confidence: {intent_metadata.intent_confidence:.2f}\n"
                f"  Ambiguity Score: {intent_metadata.ambiguity_score:.2f}"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: intent metadata.")
    
        # System metrics
        snapshot = context.get("system_snapshot")
        if snapshot:
            cpu = snapshot.get("cpu_percent", "N/A")
            mem = snapshot.get("memory", {})
            disk = snapshot.get("disk", {})
            parts.append(
                f"[SYSTEM STATE]\n"
                f"  CPU: {cpu}%\n"
                f"  Memory: {mem.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(mem.get('available', 0))} available)\n"
                f"  Disk: {disk.get('percent', 'N/A')}% used "
                f"({self._format_bytes(disk.get('free', 0))} free)"
            )
            logger.debug("Context injected: system snapshot.")
    
        # Running processes
        running = context.get("running_apps")
        if running:
            proc_list = ", ".join(running[:20])
            parts.append(f"[RUNNING APPS]\n  {proc_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d running processes.", len(running))
    
        # Foreground app
        fg_app = context.get("foreground_app")
        if fg_app:
            parts.append(f"[FOREGROUND APP]\n  {fg_app}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: foreground app = %s.", fg_app)
    
        # Open windows
        windows = context.get("open_windows")
        if windows:
            win_list = ", ".join(windows[:15])
            parts.append(f"[OPEN WINDOWS]\n  {win_list}")
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d open windows.", len(windows))
    
        # Aegis v3.1+: Daily Memory (Persistence)
        daily = context.get("daily_history")
        if daily:
            events = []
            for e in daily[-15:]:
                cat = e.get('app_category')
                cat_str = f" ({cat})" if cat else ""
                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()
E           AttributeError: 'MemoryManager' object has no attribute 'get_user_profile'

                events.append(f"  - {e['timestamp'].split('T')[1][:5]} [{e['app']}{cat_str}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}")
    
            parts.append("[DAILY HISTORY (TODAY)]\n" + "\n".join(events))
            logger.debug("Context injected: %d daily history events with categories.", len(daily))
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Past History Retrieval
        if self._memory and any(k in user_input.lower() for k in ["yesterday", "last week", "date", "202"]):
            target_date = None
            if "yesterday" in user_input.lower():
                target_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime("%Y-%m-%d")
            else:
                match = re.search(r"\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}", user_input)
                if match:
                    target_date = match.group(0)
    
            if target_date:
                past_history = self._memory.get_daily_history(target_date)
                if past_history:
                    events = [
                        f"  - [{e['app']}] {e['action_type']}: {e['command']} -> {e['result']}"
                        for e in past_history[-15:]
                    ]
                    parts.append(f"[PAST HISTORY ({target_date})]\n" + "\n".join(events))
                    logger.debug("Context injected: past history for %s.", target_date)
    
        # Aegis v3.1: Autonomous Learning & Preferences
        rejected = context.get("recent_rejected")
        learning_parts = []
    
        if rejected:
            # Analyze rejection reasons for pattern learning
            reasons = [r.get("reason", "").lower() for r in rejected if r.get("reason")]
            if any("clear" in r or "esc" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User often prefers skipping screen clearing (ESC) in Calculator/CLI.")
            if any("tab" in r or "window" in r for r in reasons):
                learning_parts.append("  - LEARNED: User prefers reusing existing tabs/windows when possible.")
    
            # Generic catch-all for recent feedback (Ultimate requirement)
            recent_feedback = [r.get("reason") for r in rejected if r.get("reason")][:3]
            for rf in recent_feedback:
                learning_parts.append(f"  - LEARNED: User previously rejected a plan because: \"{rf}\"")
    
        # Aegis v3.2: Macro Detection Logic
        if daily:
            # Count repeated commands
            from collections import Counter
            commands = [f"{e['app']}:{e['command']}" for e in daily if e['command']]
            counts = Counter(commands)
            for cmd, count in counts.items():
                if count >= 3:
                    app, val = cmd.split(":", 1)
                    learning_parts.append(f"  - MACRO SUGGESTION: User repeats '{val}' in {app} frequently ({count} times). Suggest direct macro optimization.")
    
        if learning_parts:
            parts.append("[LEARNING & PREFERENCES]\n" + "\n".join(learning_parts))
            logger.debug("Context injected: autonomous learning & macro patterns.")
    
        # Aegis v3.5: User Behavioral Profile
        if self._memory:
>           profile = self._memory.get_user_profile()
